Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Luminary 131 (Apollo 13) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 001 OF AGC PROGRAM LMY99 BY NASA 2021112-061
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

021151,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     Part of the source code for Luminary 1A build 099.

021153,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), for Apollo 11.

021158,000011:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2009-05-26 OH   Transcribed from page images.
021159,000012:                                                                                                  ##              2009-06-05 RSB  Corrected a typos.
021160,000013:                                                                                                  ##              2009-06-06 RSB  Added a missing instruction, and a block
021161,000014:                                                                                                  ##                              of 3 missing instructions.
021162,000015:                                                                                                  ##              2009-06-07 RSB  Fixed a misprint.
021163,000016:                                                                                                  ##              2009-06-07 RSB  Changed the construct "2DEC E-6 B12" 
021164,000017:                                                                                                  ##                              (which isn't legal in yaYUL) to
021165,000018:                                                                                                  ##                              "2DEC 1.0 E-6 B12".
021166,000019:                                                                                                  ##              2011-05-07 JL   Removed workarounds.
021167,000020:                                                                                                  ##              2016-12-13 RSB  GOTOP00H -> GOTOPOOH
021168,000021:                                                                                                  ##              2016-12-14 RSB  Proofed text comments with octopus/ProoferComments

021188,000041:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021189,000042: 
021190,000043:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021191,000044: 
021192,000045:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021193,000046:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021194,000047: 
021195,000048:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021196,000049: 
021197,000050:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021198,000051:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021199,000052:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021200,000053:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021201,000054: 
021202,000055:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021203,000056: 
021204,000057:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021205,000058: 
021206,000059:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021207,000060: 
021208,000061:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
021209,000062:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
021210,000063:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
021211,000064:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
021212,000065:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021213,000066:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021214,000067:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
021215,000068:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
021216,000069:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
021217,000070:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021218,000071: 
021219,000072:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021220,000073: 
021221,000074:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021222,000075:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021223,000076: 
021224,000077:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021225,000078: 
021226,000079:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021227,000080: 
021228,000081:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021229,000082: 
021230,000083:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021231,000084: 
021232,000085:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021233,000086: 
021234,000087:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021235,000088: 
021236,000089:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG.
021237,000090: 
021238,000091:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021239,000092: 
021240,000093:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
021241,000094: 
021242,000095: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021243,000096: 
021244,000097: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
021245,000098: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021246,000099: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
021247,000100: 
021248,000101: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021249,000102: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
021250,000103: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20                                
021251,000104: 24,2000           05327        PROG20             TC       2PHSCHNG

021657,000510:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021658,000511: 
021659,000512:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021660,000513:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021661,000514:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021662,000515: 
021663,000516:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021664,000517: 
021665,000518:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021666,000519:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021667,000520:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021668,000521:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021669,000522: 
021670,000523:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021671,000524: 
021672,000525:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021673,000526:

021961,000814:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021962,000815:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021963,000816: 
021964,000817:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021965,000818:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021966,000819: 
021967,000820:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021968,000821: 
021969,000822:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021970,000823:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021971,000824: 
021972,000825:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021973,000826: 
021974,000827:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021975,000828:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021976,000829: 
021977,000830:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021978,000831: 
021979,000832:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021980,000833:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021981,000834:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021982,000835:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021983,000836: 
021984,000837:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021985,000838:                                                                                                  #        
021986,000839:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021987,000840:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021988,000841: 
021989,000842:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021990,000843: 
021991,000844:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
021992,000845:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021993,000846:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021994,000847: 
021995,000848:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021996,000849: 
021997,000850:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021998,000851: 
021999,000852:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022000,000853: 
022001,000854:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
022002,000855: 
022003,000856:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022004,000857: 
022005,000858:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
022006,000859: 
022007,000860:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022008,000861:

022186,001039:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022187,001040:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022188,001041: 
022189,001042:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022190,001043:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022191,001044: 
022192,001045:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022193,001046: 
022194,001047:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022195,001048: 
022196,001049:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022197,001050: 
022198,001051:                                                                                                  #        TC      R23LEM
022199,001052: 
022200,001053:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022201,001054: 
022202,001055:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL        R61LEM
022203,001056:                                                                                                  #        SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022204,001057: 
022205,001058:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022206,001059: 
022207,001060:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1      ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022208,001061:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23
022209,001062:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF TERM WILL TERMINATE R23 +P20
022210,001063: 
022211,001064:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022212,001065: 
022213,001066:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022214,001067:

022216,001069: 
022217,001070:                                                                                                  #        N.A.
022218,001071: 
022219,001072:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED -
022220,001073: 
022221,001074:                                                                                                  #        ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)

022270,001123:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022271,001124:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022272,001125: 
022273,001126:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022274,001127:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022275,001128: 
022276,001129:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022277,001130: 
022278,001131:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022279,001132:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022280,001133:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022281,001134: 
022282,001135:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022283,001136: 
022284,001137:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
022285,001138:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
022286,001139:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
022287,001140:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
022288,001141: 
022289,001142:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022290,001143: 
022291,001144:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
022292,001145:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
022293,001146:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
022294,001147: 
022295,001148:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022296,001149: 
022297,001150:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
022298,001151:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022299,001152:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022300,001153: 
022301,001154:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022302,001155: 
022303,001156:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022304,001157: 
022305,001158:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022306,001159: 
022307,001160:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022308,001161: 
022309,001162:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022310,001163: 
022311,001164:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022312,001165: 
022313,001166:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022314,001167: 
022315,001168:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
022316,001169: 
022317,001170: 24,3206  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022318,001171: 24,3206                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022319,001172: 24,3206           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022320,001173: 24,3207           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022321,001174: 24,3210           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022322,001175: 24,3211           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21

022326,001179: 24,3215           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS

022386,001239:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
022387,001240:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION

022393,001246:

022595,001448:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                                                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022596,001449: 
022597,001450:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022598,001451: 
022599,001452:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022600,001453:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022601,001454:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022602,001455:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022603,001456:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022604,001457: 
022605,001458:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022606,001459:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022607,001460:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022608,001461:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022609,001462: 
022610,001463:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022611,001464:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022612,001465:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022613,001466:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022614,001467:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022615,001468: 
022616,001469:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022617,001470: 
022618,001471:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022619,001472:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022620,001473: 
022621,001474:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022622,001475: 
022623,001476:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022624,001477:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022625,001478:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022626,001479: 
022627,001480:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022628,001481: 
022629,001482:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022630,001483: 
022631,001484:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022632,001485: 
022633,001486:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022634,001487:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022635,001488: 
022636,001489:    4523           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND

022679,001532:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                         . IF EITHER:
022680,001533: 
022681,001534:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022682,001535:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022683,001536:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022684,001537:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022685,001538:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022686,001539:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022687,001540:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022688,001541:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022689,001542:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022690,001543:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022691,001544:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022692,001545:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022693,001546:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022694,001547:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022695,001548:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022696,001549:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022697,001550:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022698,001551:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022699,001552:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022700,001553:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022701,001554: 
022702,001555:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022703,001556: 
022704,001557:                                                                                                  #        L       TC      SETTRKF
022705,001558: 
022706,001559:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:  IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
022707,001560: 
022708,001561:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
022709,001562: 
022710,001563:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022711,001564: 
022712,001565:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL LAMP
022713,001566: 
022714,001567:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)                                                          ED.
022715,001568: 
022716,001569:    4564           34753        SETTRKF            CAF      BIT1                                  #  NO ACTION IF DURING LAMP TEST.
022717,001570:    4565           71303                           MASK     IMODES33                              
022718,001571:    4566           10000                           CCS      A                                     
022719,001572:    4567           00002                           TC       Q

022751,001604:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022752,001605: 
022753,001606:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022754,001607: 
022755,001608:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022756,001609:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022757,001610:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022758,001611:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022759,001612:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022760,001613:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022761,001614:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022762,001615:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022763,001616:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022764,001617:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022765,001618:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022766,001619:                                                                                                  #        TO TASKOVER.
022767,001620: 
022768,001621:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022769,001622:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022770,001623:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022771,001624: 
022772,001625:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022773,001626: 
022774,001627:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022775,001628: 
022776,001629:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022777,001630: 
022778,001631:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022779,001632:                                                                                                  #        
022780,001633:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022781,001634: 
022782,001635:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022783,001636: 
022784,001637:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
022785,001638: 
022786,001639: 24,3255                                           BANK     24                                    
022787,001640: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
022788,001641: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
022789,001642: 
022790,001643: 25,2062  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022791,001644: 25,2062                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
022792,001645: 25,2062           02071        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
022793,001646: 25,2063           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
022794,001647: 25,2064           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.

022800,001653:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022801,001654: 
022802,001655:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022803,001656:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022804,001657:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022805,001658:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022806,001659:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022807,001660:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022808,001661:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022809,001662:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
022810,001663:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022811,001664:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022812,001665:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022813,001666:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022814,001667:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022815,001668:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022816,001669:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022817,001670:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022818,001671: 
022819,001672:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022820,001673: 
022821,001674:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022822,001675: 
022823,001676:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022824,001677: 
022825,001678:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022826,001679: 
022827,001680:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022828,001681: 
022829,001682:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022830,001683: 
022831,001684:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022832,001685: 
022833,001686:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022834,001687: 
022835,001688: 25,2071           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
022836,001689: 25,2072           23315                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
022837,001690: 25,2073           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
022838,001691: 25,2074           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
022839,001692: 25,2075           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
022840,001693: 25,2076           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY                              
022841,001694: 25,2077           00002                           DEC      2          B-14

022876,001729:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022877,001730: 
022878,001731:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022879,001732: 
022880,001733:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022881,001734:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022882,001735:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022883,001736:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022884,001737:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022885,001738:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022886,001739:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022887,001740:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022888,001741:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022889,001742:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022890,001743:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022891,001744:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022892,001745:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022893,001746:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022894,001747:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022895,001748:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022896,001749:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022897,001750:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022898,001751:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022899,001752:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022900,001753:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022901,001754:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022902,001755: 
022903,001756:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022904,001757: 
022905,001758:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022906,001759:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022907,001760: 
022908,001761:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022909,001762: 
022910,001763:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022911,001764: 
022912,001765:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022913,001766: 
022914,001767:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022915,001768: 
022916,001769:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022917,001770: 
022918,001771:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022919,001772: 
022920,001773:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
022921,001774: 
022922,001775:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
022923,001776: 
022924,001777: 25,2127           02156        DORREPOS           TC       SETRRECR                              #  SET UP RR CDU ERROR COUNTERS.
022925,001778:

022969,001822:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                         IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
022970,001823: 
022971,001824:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
022972,001825:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022973,001826:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022974,001827:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022975,001828:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022976,001829:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022977,001830:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022978,001831:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022979,001832:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022980,001833:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022981,001834:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022982,001835:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022983,001836:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022984,001837:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022985,001838:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022986,001839:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022987,001840:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022988,001841:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022989,001842:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022990,001843:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022991,001844: 
022992,001845:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022993,001846: 
022994,001847:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022995,001848:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022996,001849:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022997,001850:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022998,001851: 
022999,001852:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023000,001853: 
023001,001854:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
023002,001855: 
023003,001856:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023004,001857: 
023005,001858:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
023006,001859:

023008,001861: 
023009,001862:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023010,001863:

023066,001919:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023067,001920: 
023068,001921:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023069,001922: 
023070,001923:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023071,001924:                                                                                                  #        RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
023072,001925:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023073,001926:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
023074,001927:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
023075,001928:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023076,001929:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023077,001930:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
023078,001931:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023079,001932:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
023080,001933:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023081,001934:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023082,001935:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023083,001936:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
023084,001937: 
023085,001938:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023086,001939:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
023087,001940:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
023088,001941:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023089,001942:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023090,001943: 
023091,001944:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023092,001945:

023159,002012:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023160,002013: 
023161,002014:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023162,002015: 
023163,002016:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023164,002017:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023165,002018:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023166,002019:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023167,002020:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023168,002021:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023169,002022:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
023170,002023:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023171,002024:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023172,002025:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023173,002026:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023174,002027:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023175,002028:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023176,002029: 
023177,002030:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023178,002031:                                                                                                  #        
023179,002032:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023180,002033:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

023269,002122:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                        R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023270,002123: 
023271,002124:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023272,002125: 
023273,002126:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023274,002127:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023275,002128:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023276,002129:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023277,002130:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023278,002131:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023279,002132:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023280,002133:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023281,002134:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023282,002135:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023283,002136:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023284,002137:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023285,002138:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023286,002139:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023287,002140:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023288,002141:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023289,002142:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023290,002143:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023291,002144:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023292,002145:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023293,002146:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023294,002147:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023295,002148: 
023296,002149:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023297,002150: 
023298,002151:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023299,002152:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
023300,002153:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023301,002154:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023302,002155: 
023303,002156:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023304,002157: 
023305,002158:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023306,002159:

023308,002161:

023310,002163:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV

023320,002173:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                         CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.

023359,002212:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023360,002213: 
023361,002214:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023362,002215:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023363,002216:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023364,002217:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023365,002218:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023366,002219:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023367,002220:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023368,002221:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023369,002222:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023370,002223:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
023371,002224:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023372,002225:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
023373,002226:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023374,002227:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023375,002228:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023376,002229:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023377,002230:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023378,002231:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023379,002232:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023380,002233:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023381,002234:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023382,002235: 
023383,002236:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023384,002237: 
023385,002238:                                                                                                  #        FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
023386,002239: 
023387,002240:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023388,002241: 
023389,002242:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, (SEE DODES)

023396,002249:
