023532,002385:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023533,002386: 
023534,002387:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023535,002388: 
023536,002389:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023537,002390:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023538,002391:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023539,002392:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023540,002393:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023541,002394:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023542,002395:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023543,002396:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023544,002397:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023545,002398:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023546,002399:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023547,002400:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023548,002401:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023549,002402:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023550,002403:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023551,002404:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023552,002405:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023553,002406:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023554,002407:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023555,002408:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023556,002409:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023557,002410:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023558,002411:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023559,002412:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023560,002413:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023561,002414: 
023562,002415:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023563,002416: 
023564,002417:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023565,002418:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023566,002419:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023567,002420: 
023568,002421:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023569,002422:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023570,002423: 
023571,002424:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023572,002425:                                                                                                  #        ENDRADAR. FINDVAC
023573,002426: 
023574,002427:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023575,002428: 
023576,002429:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023577,002430:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023578,002431: 
023579,002432:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023580,002433:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023581,002434:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023582,002435: 
023583,002436: 25,2573           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

Page 547 

023629,002482:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023630,002483: 
023631,002484:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023632,002485: 
023633,002486:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023634,002487:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023635,002488:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023636,002489:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023637,002490:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023638,002491:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023639,002492:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023640,002493:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023641,002494:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023642,002495:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023643,002496:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023644,002497:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023645,002498:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023646,002499:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023647,002500:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023648,002501:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023649,002502:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023650,002503:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023651,002504:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023652,002505:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023653,002506:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023654,002507:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023655,002508:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023656,002509:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023657,002510:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023658,002511:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023659,002512:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023660,002513:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023661,002514:                                                                                                  #        CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023662,002515:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023663,002516:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023664,002517:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023665,002518:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023666,002519:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023667,002520:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023668,002521:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023669,002522:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023670,002523: 
023671,002524:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023672,002525: 
023673,002526:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023674,002527: 
023675,002528:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:

024298,003151:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION
024299,003152:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO. 2    BY J.D. COYNE   SDC     DATE 12-7-66
024300,003153: 
024301,003154:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024302,003155:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.
024303,003156:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPUTES THE LOS VECTOR TO THE CSM, CONVERTS IT TO STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES AND STORES IT IN RRTARGET.
024304,003157:                                                                                                  #        3)      COMPUTES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR AND STORES IT IN MLOSV
024305,003158: 
024306,003159:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE      CALL
024307,003160:                                                                                                  #                                LPS20.1
024308,003161: 
024309,003162:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024310,003163:                                                                                                  #        LEMPREC, CSMPREC
024311,003164: 
024312,003165:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT_  RETURN TO CALLER + 2
024313,003166: 
024314,003167:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS_  NONE
024315,003168: 
024316,003169:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024317,003170: 
024318,003171:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT_
024319,003172:                                                                                                  #        LOS VECTOR (HALF UNIT) IN SM COORDINATES STORED IN RRTARGET
024320,003173:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR (METERS SCALED B-29) STORED IN MSLOV
024321,003174:                                                                                                  #        RRNBSW CLEARED
024322,003175: 
024323,003176:                                                                                                  #  INITIALIZED ERASEABLE
024324,003177:                                                                                                  #        TDEC1 MUST CONTAIN THE TIME FOR EXTRAPOLATION
024325,003178:                                                                                                  #        SEE ORBITAL INTEGRATION ROUTINE
024326,003179: 
024327,003180:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS_
024328,003181:                                                                                                  #        MPAC DESTROYED BY THIS ROUTINE
024329,003182: 
024330,003183: 23,2314                                           BANK     23                                    
024331,003184: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
024332,003185: 24,2000                                           BANK

Page 565 

024334,003187: 24,3255                                           COUNT*   $$/LPS20                              
024335,003188: 
024336,003189: 24,3255           43020        LPS20.1            STQ      BOFF                                  
024337,003190: 24,3256           01757                                    LS21X                                 
024338,003191: 24,3257           01343                                    LOSCMFLG                              #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS NOT CALLED BY R21
024339,003192: 24,3260           51264                                    LMINT                                 #  SO CALL LEMCONIC TO GET LM STATE
024340,003193: 24,3261           77614                           BON                                            #  IF IN R21 AND ON LUNAR SURFACE

024427,003280:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024428,003281:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
024429,003282: 
024430,003283:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024431,003284:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024432,003285:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024433,003286:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024434,003287:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024435,003288: 
024436,003289:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
024437,003290: 
024438,003291:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024439,003292:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          LPS20.1
024440,003293:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
024441,003294:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
024442,003295:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
024443,003296: 
024444,003297:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024445,003298: 
024446,003299:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024447,003300:                                                                                                  #        00001 - ERROR EXIT 1 - RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024448,003301:                                                                                                  #        00002 - ERROR EXIT 2 - RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024449,003302: 
024450,003303:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 - COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024451,003304:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024452,003305: 
024453,003306:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) - A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024454,003307:                                                                                                  #        RM - THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024455,003308: 
024456,003309:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024457,003310:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM - THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
024458,003311:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN - RR TRUNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024459,003312:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT - RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024460,003313:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,AOG - THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS
024461,003314:                                                                                                  #                MKTIME - THE TIME OF THE RR READING, DP, IN CENTISECONDS
024462,003315: 
024463,003316:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024464,003317:                                                                                                  #        RNRAD, THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 569 

024466,003319:                                                                                                  #                1) RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
024467,003320:                                                                                                  #                2) RR RANGE RATE, SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
024468,003321:                                                                                                  #        THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX, CDUY, CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
024469,003322: 
024470,003323:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:  LRS22.1X, A, L, Q, PUSHLIST

024651,003504:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                DATE - 29 MAY 1967

024653,003506:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                    ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024654,003507: 
024655,003508:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024656,003509:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024657,003510:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024658,003511:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024659,003512: 
024660,003513:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024661,003514:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024662,003515:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024663,003516:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024664,003517:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024665,003518:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024666,003519:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024667,003520: 
024668,003521:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024669,003522:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024670,003523:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RARARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024671,003524: 
024672,003525:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024673,003526:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024674,003527:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024675,003528:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024676,003529:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024677,003530:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024678,003531: 
024679,003532:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024680,003533:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024681,003534:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024682,003535:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024683,003536:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024684,003537:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024685,003538:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024686,003539:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024687,003540:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024688,003541:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024689,003542:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN ACG
024690,003543:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024691,003544:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024692,003545:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024693,003546:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024694,003547: 
024695,003548:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024696,003549:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024697,003550:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

Page 575 

024699,003552:                                                                                                  #        ULC, RXZ, SINTHETA, LGRET, RDRET, BVECTOR, W.IND, X78T
024700,003553: 
024701,003554: 13,2207                                           BANK     13

025092,003945: 
025093,003946:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025094,003947:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025095,003948:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025096,003949:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025097,003950: 
025098,003951:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025099,003952:                                                                                                  #        INSTALL         LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
025100,003953:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
025101,003954: 
025102,003955:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025103,003956:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025104,003957:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR

Page 583 

025106,003959:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
025107,003960:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025108,003961:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
025109,003962: 
025110,003963:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025111,003964:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025112,003965:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
025113,003966:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025114,003967:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025115,003968:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025116,003969:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
025117,003970:

025224,004077: 
025225,004078:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES THE RELATIVE POSITION VECTOR BETWEEN THE CSM
025226,004079:                                                                                                  #  AND THE LM, LEAVING THE UNIT VECTOR IN THE PUSHLIST AND MPAC AND THE

025252,004105:                                                                                                  #  RADARANG
025253,004106: 
025254,004107:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY

025315,004168: 
025316,004169:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025317,004170:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO 0                      BY P VOLANTE   SDC              DATE 1-15-67
025318,004171: 
025319,004172:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025320,004173: 
025321,004174:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025322,004175:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025323,004176:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025324,004177:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025325,004178: 
025326,004179:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025327,004180: 
025328,004181:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025329,004182: 
025330,004183:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC        R61LEM
025331,004184:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC        RRDESSM
025332,004185:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY        FLAGDOWN
025333,004186:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
025334,004187:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL
025335,004188: 
025336,004189:                                                                                                  #  EXIT - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
025337,004190:

025339,004192: 
025340,004193:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD (SP) - FOR DISPLAY IN R1 -     00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
025341,004194:                                                                                                  #                                                11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED

Page 594 

025571,004424:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025572,004425:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025573,004426: 
025574,004427:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025575,004428: 
025576,004429:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025577,004430:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025578,004431:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025579,004432:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025580,004433:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025581,004434:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025582,004435: 
025583,004436:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025584,004437: 
025585,004438:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025586,004439: 
025587,004440:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRTONLY
025588,004441:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025589,004442:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025590,004443:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025591,004444:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025592,004445:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025593,004446: 
025594,004447:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025595,004448: 
025596,004449:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025597,004450: 
025598,004451:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)

025801,004654:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025802,004655: 
025803,004656:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025804,004657:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025805,004658:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025806,004659:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025807,004660:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025808,004661: 
025809,004662:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025810,004663:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025811,004664: 
025812,004665: 32,2547                                           BANK     32                                    
025813,004666: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025814,004667: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025815,004668: 
025816,004669: 32,2547                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025817,004670: 32,2547  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025818,004671: 
025819,004672: 32,2547           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025820,004673: 32,2550           55107                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025821,004674: 32,2551           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025822,004675: 
025823,004676: 32,2552           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025824,004677: 32,2553           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025825,004678: 32,2554           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025826,004679: 32,2555           12563                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025827,004680: 
025828,004681: 32,2556           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025829,004682: 32,2557           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025830,004683: 32,2560           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025831,004684: 32,2561           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025832,004685: 32,2562           21102                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
025833,004686: 
025834,004687: 32,2563           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
025835,004688: 32,2564           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025836,004689: 32,2565           31102                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
025837,004690: 32,2566           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
025838,004691: 32,2567           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025839,004692: 32,2570           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025840,004693: 32,2571           12577                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
025841,004694: 
025842,004695: 32,2572           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025843,004696: 32,2573           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025844,004697: 32,2574           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025845,004698: 32,2575           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025846,004699: 32,2576           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025847,004700: 
025848,004701: 32,2577           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
025849,004702: 32,2600           12552                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
025850,004703:

Page 601 

025852,004705:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
025853,004706: 
025854,004707: 32,2601           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         
025855,004708: 32,2602           52155                           DXCH     MPAC                                  
025856,004709: 32,2603           32774                           CA       R29FXLOC                              #  = ADRES INTB15 + -34D

025860,004713: 32,2607           07532                           TC       MPACVBUF                              #  MOVE UNIT(LOS) TO AX*SR*T ARG AREA.
025861,004714:

025879,004732: 32,2630           04616                           TC       BANKCALL

025881,004734:

025885,004738:

Page 602 

025887,004740:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTE COSINE OF THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE PRESENT LOS AND THE RR BORESIGHT VECTOR, AND SET THE SELFTRACK ENABLE IF
025888,004741:                                                                                                  #  THE COSINE IS APPROXIMATELY COS(.5 DEG) OR GREATER (I.E. SMALLER ANGLE).
